</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>AstroNova Reports Fiscal 2025 Second Quarter Financial Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>Company to host conference call at 9:30 a.m. ET today </I></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Revenue of $40.5&nbsp;million, up 14.1% year over year </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

margin of 35.6%, unchanged year over year </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Operating income of $1.1&nbsp;million; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> operating income of
$2.2&nbsp;million </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Net loss per share of $(0.04) vs. $(0.22) in the second quarter of fiscal year 2024; <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> diluted earnings per share of $0.08 vs. $0.15 in the second quarter of fiscal 2024 </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Adjusted EBITDA of $3.9&nbsp;million, up 5.3% year over year </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>West Warwick, R.I., September</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;16, 2024</B> &#150; AstroNova, Inc. (Nasdaq: ALOT), a global leader in data visualization technologies,
today announced financial results for its fiscal 2025 second quarter ended August&nbsp;3, 2024. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>CEO Commentary </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We demonstrated the resilience of our Product Identification (PI) and Test&nbsp;&amp; Measurement (T&amp;M) segments during a second quarter in which we
began shipping a previously delayed order and benefited from the resolution of supply chain shortages,&#148; said Greg Woods, AstroNova&#146;s President and Chief Executive Officer. &#147;In PI, total revenue increased more than 5% year-over-year
and more than 17% sequentially, driven primarily by organic growth. T&amp;M revenue grew 37% sequentially and year-over-year, reflecting continued momentum from our Aerospace product line. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;During the quarter we began the process of integrating our May acquisition of MTEX NS. Because MTEX was an entrepreneurial, private company, the
integration got off to a slow start in the quarter, generating revenue of only $0.8&nbsp;million and an operating loss of $1.4&nbsp;million. We expect it to take through the remainder of fiscal 2025 to transition MTEX&#146;s systems, processes and
business tools to those of the AstroNova Operating System,&#148; Woods said. &#147;We remain excited about MTEX&#146;s core strengths, including its engineering and manufacturing capabilities and especially its game-changing ink and printhead
technologies. In the coming months we will be devoting additional resources to integrating that technology into more of our Product Identification products. Buoyed by several large tradeshows since the acquisition, MTEX has built a strong product
backlog that we expect to begin shipping in the third and fourth quarters, which will enable the business to meet our target revenue contribution of $8&nbsp;million to $10&nbsp;million for full-year fiscal 2025.&#148; </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Business Outlook </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Looking ahead, we are optimistic about our growth prospects,&#148; Woods continued. &#147;We are well-positioned to continue driving organic growth,
supported by our commitment to delivering innovative, high-margin products while maintaining strong cost controls. We anticipate achieving our fiscal year targets for revenue growth. As a result of the MTEX integration, we have reduced our
consolidated FY 2025 Adjusted EBITDA margin estimate to a range of 9% to 10% and expect to be within the range of 13% to 14% in fiscal 2026.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Q2
FY 2025 Financial Results </U></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Adjusted EBITDA was $3.9&nbsp;million for the second quarter of fiscal 2025, compared with $3.7&nbsp;million in the comparable period of fiscal 2024. Adjusted
EBITDA for the fiscal 2025 period excludes the impact of $1.7&nbsp;million in costs related to stock-based compensation, CFO transition and MTEX acquisition-related expenses. Adjusted EBITDA for the fiscal 2024 period excludes the impact of
stock-based compensation, retrofit and restructuring costs of $3.9&nbsp;million. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Bookings for the second quarter of fiscal 2025 were $35.8&nbsp;million
compared with $30.1&nbsp;million in the second quarter of fiscal 2024. Bookings were primarily higher in the Test and Measurement segment. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Backlog as of
August&nbsp;3, 2024, was $29.9&nbsp;million, compared with $31.6&nbsp;million at the end of the first quarter of fiscal 2025, as some shipments delayed in the first quarter were shipped in the second quarter. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Q2 FY 2025 Operating Segment Results </U></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Product
Identification </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">PI segment revenue was $27.2&nbsp;million in the second quarter of fiscal 2025, compared with $25.8&nbsp;million in the second quarter
of 2024, reflecting organic growth and the addition of MTEX NS. Segment operating profit was $2.3&nbsp;million, or 8.6% of revenue, compared with a segment operating loss of $461,000, or (1.8%) of revenue, in the same period last year. Excluding the
results of MTEX in fiscal 2025 and certain expenses in both periods (see reconciliation tables below for GAAP reconciliation), <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> operating profit was $3.6&nbsp;million, or 13.7% of revenue in the fiscal
2025 period, compared with <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> operating profit of $3.0&nbsp;million, or 11.5% of revenue, in the same period of fiscal 2024. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">2 </P>

</DIV></Center>

<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Test&nbsp;&amp; Measurement </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Test&nbsp;&amp; Measurement (T&amp;M) segment revenue was $13.4&nbsp;million in the second quarter of fiscal 2025, compared with $9.7&nbsp;million in the same
period of fiscal 2024, representing a 37.2% increase. Segment operating profit was $3.8&nbsp;million, or 28.7% of revenue, in the second quarter of fiscal 2025 compared with $1.9&nbsp;million, or 19.7% of revenue, in the second quarter of fiscal
2024. This improvement reflected higher revenue and $1.3 million in revenue and $1.0 million in operating profit related to non-recurring items. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Earnings Conference Call Information </U></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">AstroNova will
discuss its fiscal 2025 second quarter financial results in an investor conference call at 9:30 a.m. ET today. To access the conference call, please dial (833) <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">470-1428</FONT> (U.S. and Canada) or (404) <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">975-4839</FONT> (International) approximately 10 minutes prior to the start time and enter access code 381674. A real-time and an archived audio webcast of the call will be available through the &#147;Investors&#148;
section of the AstroNova website, <U>https://investors.astronovainc.com</U>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Use of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial
Measures </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In addition to financial measures prepared in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles (GAAP), this news release contains the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> gross profit, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> gross margin, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT>
operating income, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> operating margin, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> net income, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> net income (loss) per common share and Adjusted
EBITDA. AstroNova believes that the inclusion of these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures helps investors gain a meaningful understanding of changes in the Company&#146;s core operating results and can help investors
who wish to make comparisons between AstroNova and other companies on both a GAAP and a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> basis. AstroNova&#146;s management uses these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial
measures, in addition to GAAP financial measures, as the basis for measuring its core operating performance and comparing such performance to that of prior periods and to the performance of its competitors. These measures are also used by the
Company&#146;s management to assist with their financial and operating decision-making. Please refer to the financial reconciliation table included in this news release for a reconciliation of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT>
measures to the most directly comparable GAAP measures for the three months ended August&nbsp;3, 2024, and July&nbsp;29, 2023. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">AstroNova has not
reconciled the forward-looking Adjusted EBITDA growth percentage included in its 2025 financial targets and outlook to the most directly comparable forward-looking GAAP measure because this cannot be done without unreasonable effort due to the lack
of predictability regarding cost of sales, operating expenses, depreciation and amortization, and stock-based compensation. The impact of any of these items, individually or in the aggregate, may be significant. </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About AstroNova </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">AstroNova (Nasdaq: ALOT), a global leader in data visualization technologies since 1969, designs, manufactures, distributes, and services a broad range of
products that acquire, store, analyze, and present data in multiple formats. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Product Identification segment provides a wide array of digital, <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">end-to-end</FONT></FONT> product marking and identification solutions, including hardware, software, and supplies for OEMs, commercial printers, and brand owners. The Test and Measurement
segment provides products designed for airborne printing solutions, avionics, and data acquisition. Our aerospace products include flight deck printing solutions, networking hardware, and specialized aerospace-grade supplies. Our data acquisition
systems are used in research and development, flight testing, missile and rocket telemetry production monitoring, power, and maintenance applications. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">AstroNova is a member of the Russell Microcap<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> Index and the LD Micro Index (INDEXNYSEGIS: LDMICRO).
Additional information is available by visiting&nbsp;<U>https://astronovainc.com/</U>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Forward-Looking Statements </B></P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
